[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing session against the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample triggered a critical security alert for a file path traversal [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability. The Jazzer sanitizer `FilePathTraversal` detected that input archive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths containing `..` segments could lead to files being extracted outside the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash corresponds to a File Path Traversal vulnerability, as signaled by the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal`.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What happened  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, the fuzzer supplied a crafted input [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat, when processed by `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, caused the sanitizer hook in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook` to detect and reject a path that escapes the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget extraction directory via `..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The `FilePathTraversal.check` method is invoked, indicating that path [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization or validation logic in the `Expander` example allows traversal [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegments to persist.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception stacktrace shows repeated calls into overloaded `expand` methods [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`, suggesting multiple [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode paths for archive extraction share the same inadequate path-checking behavior.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer flags the first argument of file operations, pointing to a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing or incomplete check before opening or writing to output files.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for further inspection  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` – especially the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile, File[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` entrypoint at line [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m and the chain of overloads at lines [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal` – to understand the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecise conditions under which the sanitizer is triggered.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any utility methods within the `Expander` example that construct or normalize [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile paths before extracting archive entries.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` only serves as the entry[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint for driving the example with fuzzed data; root cause investigation should [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfocus on the `Expander` logic and its interaction with file paths.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:68[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m76[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        final boolean nullTarget = targetDirectory == null;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:        final Path targetDirPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:        T nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:            final Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:83[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises in the default `resolveIn` implementation in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry`. The method first normalizes the raw entry name to check for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m segments, but then returns a second path built from the decoded [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname without normalization or a re-check. An attacker can embed URL-encoded [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `%2e%2e/`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggering `[0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myield `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m…`, bypassing the initial safety check and causing [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to operate on an unsafe path.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method:  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Remove the two‐step resolve+normalize for raw name followed by a blind [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve of the decoded name.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Decode the entry name first [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith fallback to the raw name on decoding [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Perform a single `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and enforce the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check exactly once on the normalized path.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Return the normalized, validated `Path`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Pseudocode for replacement:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Decode name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfallback to raw name on errors[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String rawName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String decodedName;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawName, [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m invalid encoding – treat as raw[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = rawName;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Resolve and normalize[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final Path target = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Enforce no escape from parentPath[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecodedName, target[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return target;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach prevents any path segment [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from surviving normalization [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter decoding.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves the intended behavior of decoding percent-encoded entry names [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen valid, and immediately rejecting any path that would land outside [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing extraction logic in `Expander` already calls `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget directory; aligning `resolveIn` with a single, atomic normalize+check step [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures consistent safety.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, tests, or external libraries are modified. Archive expansion [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance is unchanged aside from minimal extra decode/normalize overhead.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Decoding now occurs prior to normalization for every entry. In rare cases of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-ASCII or invalid percent-encoding, the fallback to the raw name retains [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal behavior.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any existing tests that relied on the deprecated two‐step logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill continue to pass, as valid entry names without traversal segments resolve [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentically.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure comprehensive unit tests cover:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • entries with simple names  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • entries with percent-encoded safe names  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • entries with percent-encoded traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%2e%2e/`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to assert an [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException`.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         “..[35m/[0m” sequences. A patch was proposed in `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` to URL-decode     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entry names before normalization and tighten the traversal check. When building     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         after the patch, the Java compiler failed with an error in `ArchiveEntry.java`      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m“variable decodedName might already have been assigned”[1m)[0m, and the project did not  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         compile.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - During fuzz testing of `Expander.expand`, Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         flagged a critical security issue: an archive entry name containing                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m” allowed traversal outside the intended output directory    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m…[35m/output/q/r/s/[0m[95mt[0m`.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The stack trace shows the failure in `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, which  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intercepts calls to file APIs in the Expander example [1m([0m`Expander.expand`[1m)[0m,          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         indicating a zip-slip vulnerability upstream of the sanitizer.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Important Observations                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer input caused resolution of a path containing “..” segments that        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalized back outside the parent target directory.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The sanitizer [1m([0min Jazzer[1m)[0m caught the issue automatically, demonstrating that the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive-expansion logic does not properly enforce directory constraints.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The patch modifies `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m` [1m([0min                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`[1m)[0m:           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. Renames `[1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` return value from `name` to `rawName`.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Attempts to URL-decode `rawName` into `decodedName`, falling back to `rawName` [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         on decode errors.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Resolves `decodedName` against `parentPath`, normalizes it, and throws         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `IOException` if the resulting `target` does not start with `parentPath`.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The diff context around line [1;36m76[0m shows removal of the old logic [1m([0mdirect            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         resolve+normalize[1m)[0m and insertion of the try/catch wrapping `URLDecoder.decode`.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Application Result                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Maven compilation failed with:                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           `[35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiv[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95meEntry.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m84[0m,[1;36m13[0m[1m][0m variable decodedName might already have been assigned`          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The build log confirms a single compilation error, indicating a Java              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         scoping/assignment issue in the newly inserted code. The project did not build due  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to this error.                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The implementation of `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`, especially variable scoping       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         around `decodedName`, to correct the compilation error.                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - All code paths that handle entry names with special or encoded characters—e.g.,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         other archive formats or legacy APIs that bypass this method.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The interaction between `Expander.expand` [1m([0mwhich calls `resolveIn`[1m)[0m and any       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lower-level I/O calls to ensure consistent enforcement of directory constraints.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The broader archive expansion logic in `Expander.java` to identify any remaining  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unguarded resolution operations.                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
